--- Commit Message ---
LU-18858 tests: trim tmpfs when used for ZFS

to release unused ram consumed by ZFS images in /tmp,
trim ZFS pools from wait_delete_completed().
for tmpfs it's cheap and saves a lot of memory:
upto 6GBs in sanity.

Test-Parameters: fstype=zfs testlist=sanity
Signed-off-by: Alex Zhuravlev <bzzz@whamcloud.com>
Change-Id: Ib210814d2d8a5d776ea364a3528e0661ab2ae26d
